The GT numerical expression is:
`-0.459914680311301*v*(1 - v**2) - 1.87329057400732*v - 2.49934616662645*x*(0.0579034145056311*t + 1) - 2.49934616662645*x`

Let me expand this:
- `-0.459914680311301*v + 0.459914680311301*v**3 - 1.87329057400732*v - 2.49934616662645*0.0579034145056311*x*t - 2.49934616662645*x - 2.49934616662645*x`

Simplifying:
- v terms: `(-0.459914680311301 - 1.87329057400732)*v = -2.33320525431862*v`
- v³ term: `0.459914680311301*v**3`
- x terms: `-2.49934616662645*x - 2.49934616662645*x = -4.9986923332529*x`
- x*t term: `-2.49934616662645*0.0579034145056311*x*t = -0.144729688498836*x*t`

So GT = `-4.9986923332529*x - 2.33320525431862*v + 0.459914680311301*v**3 - 0.144729688498836*x*t`

The GT has basis functions: **x, v, v³, x·t** (and no constant term, i.e., constant = 0).

Now let me check each candidate for whether it can match these basis functions exactly.

**Key requirement:** The candidate must be able to express exactly: `A*x + B*v + C*v³ + D*x*t` with appropriate constants, and nothing else.

For candidates with `sin(c*t + d)` or `cos(c*t + d)` terms multiplied by x: these are `x*sin(c*t+d)` which equals `x*sin(d)*cos(c*t) + x*cos(d)*sin(c*t)`. The GT needs `x*t`, which is NOT equivalent to `x*sin(c*t)` for any constants. However, if we could set c5=0, then `x*sin(c5*t + c6) = x*sin(c6)` which is just a constant times x - we lose the t-dependence. We need `x*t` but `sin` cannot produce `x*t` exactly.

Wait - let me reconsider. Can `x*sin(c*t)` with small c approximate `x*c*t`? No - we need EXACT equivalence, not approximation.

So any candidate relying on `sin` or `cos` to capture the `x*t` term CANNOT match.

Similarly, `exp(c*t)` cannot produce `x*t`.

Candidates that could potentially match need an explicit `x*t` term or equivalent. Let me check if any candidate has this... None of the candidates have an explicit `x*t` term.

Let me verify: every single candidate uses either `sin`, `cos`, `exp`, `Abs`, `log`, `tanh`, `Max`, polynomial terms, etc. None has a bare `x*t` product.

Since the GT requires an `x*t` cross-term and none of the candidates can produce this exactly (trigonometric, exponential, and other nonlinear functions of t cannot equal a linear function of t), none of the candidates can match.

Let me double-check candidates without any t-dependence (like candidates 36, 37, 43, 46, 49, etc.) - these clearly can't match since GT has t-dependence.

And candidates with t-dependence through sin/cos/exp cannot produce the linear `x*t` term exactly.
